	<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready((function(){
		var sc = {userId: null, token: null, refreshToken:null, idToken:null};
	
		function initStorage(){
			sc.userId = sso.idTokenParsed.sub;
			sc.token = sso.token;
			sc.refreshToken = sso.refreshToken;
			sc.idToken = sso.idToken;
			localStorage.sc = JSON.stringify(sc);
		}
	
		var loadProfile = function () {
			initStorage();
			if (sso.idToken) {
				var userMail = Cookies.get('ssoMail');
				if(userMail==null){
					Cookies.set('ssoMail',sso.idTokenParsed.email, {path:"/"});
				}	
				var test = "";
				
				$("#login").addClass("hide");
				$("[data-username]").prepend(sso.idTokenParsed.name);
				$("#account,#username,#username-tooltip").removeClass("hide");
			} else {
				loadProfile();
			}
		}
	
		var checkProfile = function (authenticated) {
			if (authenticated) {
				sso.updateToken(30)
				.success(loadProfile)
				.error(function(errorData) {
					console.error('Failed to load data. ' + JSON.stringify(errorData));
				});
			} else {
				$("#login").removeClass("hide");
			}
		}
	
		var data = function(authenticated) {
			checkProfile(authenticated);
			sso.success = true;
		}
	
		if (localStorage.sc == undefined) {
			sso.init({onLoad : 'check-sso'})
			.success(data)
			.error(function(errorData) {
				console.error('Failed login. ' + JSON.stringify(errorData));
			});
		} else {
			sso.init({
				  token: $.parseJSON(localStorage.sc).token,
				  refreshToken: $.parseJSON(localStorage.sc).refreshToken,
				  idToken: $.parseJSON(localStorage.sc).idToken
			}).success(data)
			  .error(function(errorData) {
				  console.error('Failed get logged user. ' + JSON.stringify(errorData));
			});
		}
	
	})());
	</script>
